Utility functions for byte-\/swapping. Used by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___c_chunk_data_parser}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+C\+Chunk\+Data\+Parser}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aa1769ee466fd07659d8c7ef5ac61cd49}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aa1769ee466fd07659d8c7ef5ac61cd49}} 
\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAE\_EAudioBufferLengthNative@{AAE\_EAudioBufferLengthNative}}
\index{AAE\_EAudioBufferLengthNative@{AAE\_EAudioBufferLengthNative}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AAE\_EAudioBufferLengthNative}{AAE\_EAudioBufferLengthNative}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aa1769ee466fd07659d8c7ef5ac61cd49}{A\+A\+E\+\_\+\+E\+Audio\+Buffer\+Length\+Native}}}



Processing buffer length definitions for Native A\+AX hosts. 

All A\+AX Native plug-\/ins must support variable buffer lengths. The buffer lengths that a host will use are constrained by the values in this enum. All Native buffer lengths will be powers of two, as per \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ada5e011bdfdc6a996de752662b3dfbe7}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Audio\+Buffer\+Length}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ab5677b173ad8647c24d34d28272d11fc}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Data\+In\+Port\+Type}}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_component_descriptor_a230293b9f6bb413626cd487ca501df75}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Component\+Descriptor\+::\+Add\+Data\+In\+Port()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Unbuffered@{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Unbuffered}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Unbuffered@{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Unbuffered}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ab5677b173ad8647c24d34d28272d11fca43dc59a68b369ee607f70700bfd02c2d}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ab5677b173ad8647c24d34d28272d11fca43dc59a68b369ee607f70700bfd02c2d}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Data\+In\+Port\+Type\+\_\+\+Unbuffered&Data port is unbuffered; the most recently posted packet is always delivered to the alg proc \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Buffered@{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Buffered}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Buffered@{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Buffered}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ab5677b173ad8647c24d34d28272d11fcaa9f089bb87161125a38706c81ec522e0}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ab5677b173ad8647c24d34d28272d11fcaa9f089bb87161125a38706c81ec522e0}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Data\+In\+Port\+Type\+\_\+\+Buffered&Data port is buffered both on the host and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_d_s_p}{D\+SP}} and packets are updated to the current timestamp with every alg proc call

Data delivered to alg proc always reflects the latest posted packet that has a timestamp at or before the current processing buffer \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Incremental@{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Incremental}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Incremental@{AAX\_eDataInPortType\_Incremental}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ab5677b173ad8647c24d34d28272d11fca4c356b21e878cfafca33ff61e1044b2e}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ab5677b173ad8647c24d34d28272d11fca4c356b21e878cfafca33ff61e1044b2e}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Data\+In\+Port\+Type\+\_\+\+Incremental&Data port is buffered both on the host and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_d_s_p}{D\+SP}} and packets are updated only once per alg proc call \begin{DoxyVerb}Since only one packet is delivered at a time, all packets will be delivered to the alg proc unless
an internal buffer overflow occurs

@note If multiple packets are posted to this port \em before the initial call to the alg proc, only
the latest packet will be delivered to the first call to the alg proc. Thereafter, all packets will
be delivered incrementally.

@compatibility Supported in Pro Tools 12.5 and higher; when \ref AAX_eDataInPortType_Incremental is
not supported the port will be treated as \ref AAX_eDataInPortType_Unbuffered
\end{DoxyVerb}

\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_EHostLevel@{AAX\_EHostLevel}}
\index{AAX\_EHostLevel@{AAX\_EHostLevel}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AAX\_EHostLevel}{AAX\_EHostLevel}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a2d34e7a7c2e6f4f6361555ad02869219}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Host\+Level}}}



Host levels. 

Some A\+AX software hosts support different levels which are sold as separate products. For example, there may be an entry-\/level version of a product as well as a full version.

The level of a host may impact the user experience, workflows, or the availability of certain plug-\/ins. For example, some entry-\/level hosts are restricted to loading only specific plug-\/ins.

Typically an A\+AX plug-\/in should not need to query this information or change its behavior based on the level of the host.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92d}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92d}} 
\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_EMidiGlobalNodeSelectors@{AAX\_EMidiGlobalNodeSelectors}}
\index{AAX\_EMidiGlobalNodeSelectors@{AAX\_EMidiGlobalNodeSelectors}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AAX\_EMidiGlobalNodeSelectors}{AAX\_EMidiGlobalNodeSelectors}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92d}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Midi\+Global\+Node\+Selectors}}}



The Global M\+I\+DI Node Selectors. 

These selectors are used in the {\itshape channel\+Mask} argument of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_component_descriptor_a6284dda9ccca898e33075de29dad4e39}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Component\+Descriptor\+::\+Add\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_effect_descriptor_aa7709de005e0256feb522758ccc5b582}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Effect\+Descriptor\+::\+Add\+Control\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node()}} to request one or more kinds of global data. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eMIDIClick@{AAX\_eMIDIClick}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eMIDIClick@{AAX\_eMIDIClick}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92da07f7ef0ac806b94f96cc14e81678b84a}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92da07f7ef0ac806b94f96cc14e81678b84a}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Click&Selector to request click messages. The click messages are special 2-\/byte messages encoded as follows\+: \begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Accented click\+: Note on pitch 0 ({\ttfamily 0x90 0x00}) \item Unaccented click\+: Note on pitch 1 ({\ttfamily 0x90 0x01}) \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
No {\itshape  Note Off } messages are ever sent. This isn\textquotesingle{}t up-\/to-\/spec M\+I\+DI data, just a way of encoding click events. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eMIDIMtc@{AAX\_eMIDIMtc}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eMIDIMtc@{AAX\_eMIDIMtc}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92da29d1a888ea18fe3f32c7231ceb964e61}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92da29d1a888ea18fe3f32c7231ceb964e61}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Mtc&Selector to request M\+I\+DI Time Code (M\+TC) data. The Standard M\+I\+DI Time Code format. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eMIDIBeatClock@{AAX\_eMIDIBeatClock}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eMIDIBeatClock@{AAX\_eMIDIBeatClock}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92da7345d01457a861d2acb2e91d5669b803}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a349dae6bc64bda67a5440cbc6637f92da7345d01457a861d2acb2e91d5669b803}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Beat\+Clock&Selector to request M\+I\+DI Beat Clock (M\+BC) messages. This includes Song Position Pointer, Start/\+Stop/\+Continue, and Midi Clock (F8). \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4}} 
\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_EMIDINodeType@{AAX\_EMIDINodeType}}
\index{AAX\_EMIDINodeType@{AAX\_EMIDINodeType}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AAX\_EMIDINodeType}{AAX\_EMIDINodeType}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node\+Type}}}



M\+I\+DI node types. 

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_component_descriptor_a6284dda9ccca898e33075de29dad4e39}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Component\+Descriptor\+::\+Add\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalInput@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalInput}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalInput@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalInput}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4ae57de2b04978fe2e75f5bdeb034bda44}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4ae57de2b04978fe2e75f5bdeb034bda44}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node\+Type\+\_\+\+Local\+Input&Local M\+I\+DI input. \begin{DoxyVerb}\details
Local MIDI input nodes receive MIDI by accessing \ref AAX_CMidiStream buffers filled with MIDI
messages. These buffers of MIDI data are available within the algorithm context with data
corresponding to the current audio buffer being computed. The Effect can step through this
buffer like a "script" to respond to MIDI events within the audio callback.

\legacy Corresponds to RTAS Buffered MIDI input nodes in the legacy SDK
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalOutput@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalOutput}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalOutput@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_LocalOutput}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4acc1b5f2109c508b20a65b5e0fdcd643f}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4acc1b5f2109c508b20a65b5e0fdcd643f}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node\+Type\+\_\+\+Local\+Output&Local M\+I\+DI output. \begin{DoxyVerb}\details
Local MIDI output nodes send MIDI by filling buffers with MIDI messages.  Messages posted to
MIDI output nodes will be available in the host as MIDI streams, routable to MIDI track inputs
and elsewhere.

Data posted to a MIDI output buffer will be timed to correspond with the current audio buffer
being processed.  MIDI outputs support custom timestamping relative to the first sample of the
audio buffer.

The delivery of variable length SysEx messages is also supported. There are no buffer size
limitations for output of SysEx messages.

To post a MIDI output buffer, an Effect must construct a series of \ref AAX_CMidiPacket objects
and place them in the output buffer provided in the port's \ref AAX_CMidiStream

\legacy Corresponds to RTAS Buffered MIDI output nodes in the legacy SDK
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Global@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Global}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Global@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Global}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4a2be91828f8c1dac20ab5dff136fc1fce}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4a2be91828f8c1dac20ab5dff136fc1fce}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node\+Type\+\_\+\+Global&Global M\+I\+DI node. \begin{DoxyVerb}\details
Global MIDI nodes allow an Effect to receive streaming global MIDI data like MIDI Time Code,
MIDI Beat Clock, and host-specific message formats such as the Click messages used in Pro Tools.

The specific kind of data that will be received by a Global MIDI node is specified using a mask
of \ref AAX_EMidiGlobalNodeSelectors values.

Global MIDI nodes are like local MIDI nodes, except they do not show up as assignable outputs in
the host. Instead the MIDI data is automatically routed to the plug-in, without the user making
any connections.

The buffer of data provided via a Global MIDI node may be shared between all currently active
Effect instances, and this node may include both explicitly requested data and data not requested
by the current Effect. For example, if one plug-in requests MTC and another plug-in requests
Click, all plug-ins connected to this global node will get both MTC and Click messages in the
shared buffer.

\legacy Corresponds to RTAS Shared Buffer global nodes in the legacy SDK
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Transport@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Transport}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Transport@{AAX\_eMIDINodeType\_Transport}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4ac2ff856aec0724907dfd95b8e3ccbc20}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a5e1dffce35d05990dbbad651702678e4ac2ff856aec0724907dfd95b8e3ccbc20}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+M\+I\+D\+I\+Node\+Type\+\_\+\+Transport&Transport node. \begin{DoxyVerb}\details
Call \ref AAX_IMIDINode::GetTransport() on this node to access the \ref AAX_ITransport interface. 
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a47756e0a56d00468b7045eb26500cb78}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_a47756e0a56d00468b7045eb26500cb78}} 
\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_EModifiers@{AAX\_EModifiers}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AAX\_ENotificationEvent}{AAX\_ENotificationEvent}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_afab5ea2cfd731fc8f163b6caa685406e}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Notification\+Event}}}



Events I\+Ds for A\+AX notifications. 


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Notifications listed with {\itshape Sent by\+: Host} are dispatched by the A\+AX host and may be received in one or more of
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_a_c_f_effect_parameters_aa3eaeb292d2ca84086a5a058171994fd}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Effect\+Parameters\+::\+Notification\+Received()}} \item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_a_c_f_effect_g_u_i_a11a15162cb3c7019d1fabf2994fba6c6}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Effect\+G\+U\+I\+::\+Notification\+Received()}} \item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_a_c_f_effect_direct_data___v2_a741ad6f48a2fbf80ff062b1ce16bc3ab}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Effect\+Direct\+Data\+::\+Notification\+Received()}}\end{DoxyItemize}
The host will choose which components are registered to receive each event type. See the documentation for each event type for more information.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
All \textquotesingle{}A\+X\+\_\+\+\_\+\textquotesingle{} four-\/char I\+Ds are reserved for the A\+AX specification 
\end{DoxyNote}

A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Notification\+Event\+\_\+\+Delay\+Compensation\+State&The host\textquotesingle{}s delay compensation state has changed. This notification refers to the host\textquotesingle{}s delay compensation feature as a whole, rather than the specific delay compensation state for the plug-\/in.

Possible values\+: 0 (disabled), 1 (enabled)

Plug-\/ins may need to monitor the host\textquotesingle{}s delay compensation state because, while delay compensation is disabled, the host will never change the plug-\/in\textquotesingle{}s accounted latency and, therefore, will never dispatch \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_afab5ea2cfd731fc8f163b6caa685406ea06ab4b075ecb523d0dde3ec19b76a756}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Notification\+Event\+\_\+\+Signal\+Latency\+Changed}} to the plug-\/in following a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_controller_af2c648879419d94971c1308d8698601f}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Controller\+::\+Set\+Signal\+Latency()}}.

\textbackslash{}compatibility Supported in Pro Tools 12.\+6 and higher

{\itshape Data\+: {\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t}} ~\newline
 {\itshape Sent by\+: Host} \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_NoiseFloorChanged@{AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_NoiseFloorChanged}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_NoiseFloorChanged@{AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_NoiseFloorChanged}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_afab5ea2cfd731fc8f163b6caa685406eade0750c56040f18da04cf5de184c908e}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_afab5ea2cfd731fc8f163b6caa685406eade0750c56040f18da04cf5de184c908e}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Notification\+Event\+\_\+\+Noise\+Floor\+Changed&The plug-\/in\textquotesingle{}s noise floor level. The notification data is the new absolute noise floor level generated by the plug-\/in, as amplitude. For example, a plug-\/in generating a noise floor at -\/80 dB (amplitude) would provide 0.\+0001 in the notification data.

Signal below the level of the plug-\/in\textquotesingle{}s noise floor may be ignored by host features such as Dynamic Plug-\/\+In Processing, which detect whether or not there is any signal being generated by the plug-\/in

{\itshape Data\+: {\ttfamily double}} ~\newline
 {\itshape Sent by\+: Plug-\/in} \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_PriorSettingsInvalid@{AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_PriorSettingsInvalid}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_PriorSettingsInvalid@{AAX\_eNotificationEvent\_PriorSettingsInvalid}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_afab5ea2cfd731fc8f163b6caa685406ea40644990a3de0fec1f25929b535f7760}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_afab5ea2cfd731fc8f163b6caa685406ea40644990a3de0fec1f25929b535f7760}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Notification\+Event\+\_\+\+Prior\+Settings\+Invalid&Previously-\/saved settings may no longer restore the captured state. Use this notification when a change occurs which may cause a different state to be restored by saved settings, and in particular by a saved setting representing the plug-\/in\textquotesingle{}s state just prior to the change.

For example, a plug-\/in which restricts certain types of state changes when the host is in \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aa3c8056a6ce601cc3367cb7d4478e9daa83555a8ed532fa43f3583af95ca3d39b}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Host\+Mode\+Bits\+\_\+\+Live}} mode should post an \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_afab5ea2cfd731fc8f163b6caa685406ea40644990a3de0fec1f25929b535f7760}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Notification\+Event\+\_\+\+Prior\+Settings\+Invalid}} notification when this part of the plug-\/in state is changed manually by the user; if plug-\/in settings captured prior to this manual change are later set on the plug-\/in while the host is in live mode then some part of the settings change will be blocked and the captured state will not be perfectly restored.

\textbackslash{}compatibility Supported in Venue 5.\+6 and higher

{\itshape Data\+: none} ~\newline
 {\itshape Sent by\+: Plug-\/in} \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AAX\_ePageTable\_UseAlternateControl@{AAX\_ePageTable\_UseAlternateControl}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_ePageTable\_UseAlternateControl@{AAX\_ePageTable\_UseAlternateControl}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aa169208a2ce713fa021e20deb2eaf608a1a0d975a333d3aee81b22f878697e9c4}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aa169208a2ce713fa021e20deb2eaf608a1a0d975a333d3aee81b22f878697e9c4}} 
A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Page\+Table\+\_\+\+Use\+Alternate\+Control&Description of whether an alternate parameter should be used for a given slot. For example, some control surfaces support Q/\+Slope encoders. Using an alternate control mechanism, plug-\/ins mapped to these devices can assign a different slope control to the alternate slot and have it coexist with a Q control for each band. This is only applicable when mapping separate parameters to the same encoder; if the Q and Slope controls are implemented as the same parameter object in the plug-\/in then customization is not needed.

Possible response values are listed in \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_abbcc8b4e8207262a5dd9e32047a51a29}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Use\+Alternate\+Control}}

\textbackslash{}legacy converted from {\ttfamily e\+Digi\+\_\+\+Page\+Table\+\_\+\+Use\+Alternate\+Control} in the legacy S\+DK \\

\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_EPlugInCategory@{AAX\_EPlugInCategory}}
\index{AAX\_EPlugInCategory@{AAX\_EPlugInCategory}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AAX\_EPlugInCategory}{AAX\_EPlugInCategory}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aef9637518fb1ac0e2f403444c73aba4a}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Plug\+In\+Category}}}



Effect category definitions. 

Used with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_effect_descriptor_aeb6683e6758f7eb00f87c153e4809641}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Effect\+Descriptor\+::\+Add\+Category()}} to categorize an Effect.

These values are bitwise-\/exclusive and may be used in a bitmask to define multiple categories\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{myCategory = \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aef9637518fb1ac0e2f403444c73aba4aad84edabff7d1d8732079b467c07dedcc}{AAX\_ePlugInCategory\_EQ}} | \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_aef9637518fb1ac0e2f403444c73aba4aa1e8d5202983c58aa0346a9a547f55bd9}{AAX\_ePlugInCategory\_Dynamics}};}
\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The host may handle plug-\/ins with different categories in different manners, e.\+g. replacing \char`\"{}analyze\char`\"{} with \char`\"{}reverse\char`\"{} for offline processing of delays and reverbs.

The A\+AX host may associate certain plug-\/in display strings with these identifiers.

These values may be used as a bitmask, so e.\+g. a particular Effect may declare compatibility with {\ttfamily A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Sample\+Rate\+Mask\+\_\+44100 $\vert$ A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Sample\+Rate\+Mask\+\_\+48000}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ad8af5ef008b2bd478add9a0acb0a1d85}\label{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ad8af5ef008b2bd478add9a0acb0a1d85}} 
\index{AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}!AAX\_EStemFormat@{AAX\_EStemFormat}}
\index{AAX\_EStemFormat@{AAX\_EStemFormat}!AAX\_Enums.h@{AAX\_Enums.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AAX\_EStemFormat}{AAX\_EStemFormat}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___enums_8h_ad8af5ef008b2bd478add9a0acb0a1d85}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+Stem\+Format}}}



Stem format definitions. 

A stem format combines a channel count with a semantic meaning for each channel. Usually this is the speaker or speaker position associated with the data in the channel. The meanings of each channel in each stem format (i.\+e. channel orders) are listed below.

Not all stem formats are supported by all A\+AX plug-\/in hosts. An effect may describe support for any stem format combination which it supports and the host will ignore any configurations which it cannot support.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
When defining stem format support in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_a_a_x___i_host_processor}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+Host\+Processor}} effects do not use stem format properties or values. Instead, use \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___properties_8h_a13e384f22825afd3db6d68395b79ce0da00ed3da39077c52ef259f350837fc981}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Property\+\_\+\+Number\+Of\+Inputs}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___properties_8h_a13e384f22825afd3db6d68395b79ce0dab7e07d482d3b6e527fc13bbc9f4eaf63}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Property\+\_\+\+Number\+Of\+Outputs}} with integer channel count values.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
-\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___properties_8h_a13e384f22825afd3db6d68395b79ce0dadebf03028b758123965a8b988fa2df99}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Property\+\_\+\+Input\+Stem\+Format}} 

-\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___properties_8h_a13e384f22825afd3db6d68395b79ce0da211fdc6277e7fa652b5d482e810b0bc9}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Property\+\_\+\+Output\+Stem\+Format}} 

-\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{_a_a_x___properties_8h_a13e384f22825afd3db6d68395b79ce0da33a950bc2e02d38fc3be0a0ad8cc89b1}{A\+A\+X\+\_\+e\+Property\+\_\+\+Hybrid\+Input\+Stem\+Format}}
